#if 0

    !!!!!ATTENTION!!!!!
    If you are reading this, then you are probably trying to add a new code marker value.
    You've come to the right place! Follow the format carefully and add your new value
    in the appropriate place. If you need help, please contact the 'codemark' alias.

    If you are creating a new SECTION, it is imperative that you update the wiki page
    http://devdiv/sites/wikis/perf/Wiki%20Pages/CodeMarker%20Assigned%20Ranges.aspx
    claiming the range. This helps to prevent range collisions.

    Feel free to join and use the 'codemark' alias to discuss CodeMarker usage.

    Always enclose your SECTION in a conditional (just follow the established pattern)
    This is important to avoid bloat in managed assemblies that include the code marker
    enumeration. Also, please include a contact alias for the range.


    As you can probably tell this is unusual looking source code. That's because this file
    is preprocessed several times to generate C++, C# and VB sources. It's also used to
    generate a look-up-table for the CodeMarkerSink utility and a manifest for ETW events.

    This file is preprocessed by the build scripts using the C++ preprocessor with
    language-specific header files containing the #defines for the following macros:

    REM                     A simple one-line comment
    SECTION                 A more obvious comment
    NAMESPACE(x)            Beginning of a namespace declaration
    END_NAMESPACE(x)        End of a namespace
    ENUM(x)                 Beginning of an enum
    ENUMVALUE(value,name)   Enum value
    ENUMVALUEEX(value,name,metadata)   Enum value with metadata
    END_ENUM(x)             End of an enum
    CONDITIONAL(x)          Conditional compilation section: #if x
    END_CONDITIONAL(x)      End of conditional compilation
    CONDITIONAL2(x,y)       Conditional compilation secition: #if x || y
    END_CONDITIONAL2(x,y)   End of conditional compilation
    CPPONLY                 Beginning of C++ only section
    END_CPPONLY             End of C++ only section
    INTERNAL                Modifier indicating an internal class or enum
    DOCCOMMNET(x)           Developer documentation for the following enum value
#endif
